parasocial | adjective

denoting a relationship characterized by a one-sided, unreciprocated sense of intimacy felt by a fan or follower for a well-known or prominent figure (typically a media celebrity), in which the fan or follower comes to feel that they know the celebrity as a friend: a lot of parasocial relationships tend to give fans the feeling of ownership over the creator | people form parasocial bonds with characters that they see on TV.

Chapter 1: The Invitation

Louis Teo sat in his dimly lit workshop, surrounded by half-finished prototypes and scattered blueprints. The hum of machinery was a comforting background noise, but tonight, it was interrupted by an unexpected message on his screen: an invitation to a technology conference.

#adviceüó£Ô∏è

Dear kpop post spammers,

We get it. There are some kpop idols out there that really hype you and make you feel you can do anything. Idols that speak to your soul. Idols that make you just want to share about them with everyone you know.

Still, it is hard for most people to share the same feelings as you when it comes out of context in the form of a confession post, and I speak for most of us in saying that the recent flood of kpop posts has gotten out of hand. For you, the kpop idols carry deep and powerful meanings, for the rest of us, it is a large wall of text that is obstructive and annoying to scroll through. You could literally just say "check out XXX idol he/she is üî•üî•" and it would be so much better than spamming the entire chunk of text here.

So either:
1) you really love the idol

2) you are a troll that delights in making the lives of the smu community miserable as we have to take extra effort to scroll through a post that you know we will never bother to read

3) you are in a really bad situation right now and the idols you share about are your only avenue of comfort. In which case, I'm sorry to hear that you are going through this, but there are better ways and outlets of expressing your feelings.

In any case, please stop spamming kpop posts in this page. Thank you ‚ù§Ô∏è‚ù§Ô∏è
